< Rate>
5</Rate>
< review>
A regular spot for me and my coworkers. Nice selection of lunch specials. Even to go, the lunch special was packaged with care, separately and in a way to protect the bag (fork was wrapped in a to go menu, which is nice double duty for protection and advertising), the food and the flavors. Even a couple hrs later, since the food was compartmentalized, the food was still like it was at the restaurant, the salad was package neatly with the dressing on the side (in a container). Crispy and fresh. Not like at other restaurants where, although they are in a divided to go container, the food spills over, and mixes flavors. And the salad is packed with the warm food, causing it to wilt and soften. All in all, a great place to eat.</review>

< Text>
As Italian food goes, the food is a cut above nearby Don Antonio, or Il Forniao or Jason's. Quite excellent. I had not known that Bolognese sauce is supposed to have carrot in it, that you can taste. The waiter explained this to us after we asked what was in it, because we found it so delicious and interesting. The service is relaxed and friendly, very nice. I have one major complaint though. In the inside dining room when we were there, which was at the beginning of dinner service, maybe 5:30 or 6, there was a really loud noise happening from some machinery in the kitchen. It was constant and very distracting. In the patio out front it was quieter and nicer. If you go, see if you can get a seat in the front patio. They should really do something about the noise. In addition to the machinery noise, the music they were playing in the kitchen was at about the same volume as the music playing in the dining room, so the sound experience was terrible. Only one star off though, because it's otherwise such a special place.</Text>

< Review>
Well this is the first time that I've gone to Tacos Mexico. I found myself on the road headed home and wanted to eat. But I did not want to eat my regular burger or fast food. I just happened to be passing by Taco Mexico next to the entrance to the Highway 15 South so I decide to go there and get a couple tacos. I noticed that the tacos were a little small so I got a burrito to go along with it. The people that work there were friendly and courteous I received my taco my burrito and some green sauce and some napkins and my soda. All I can say the food tasted great to me I had no complaints at all. And I invite everyone in the area. I would invite everyone in the area to give it a try. Good things come in small packages and restaurants it appears. Enjoy
Oh the only reason that I gave a Taco Mexico 4 out of 5 Stars was that the whole time I was there I was a bit cold I think the air conditioner was on and it was still just know just a little bit cold for me otherwise I enjoy the whole time I was there. And the bathroom was clean.

Amos Johnson jr.
From Rosamond California< /Review>
